/****** Object:  View [dbo].[Planing_Board_Details]    Script Date: 03/18/2019 17:23:12 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[Planing_Board_Details]
AS
SELECT     dbo.PlanTable.MachineNo, dbo.PlanTable.TaskDate, dbo.PlanTable.OrderID, dbo.Buyer.BuyerName, dbo.Style.StyleName, dbo.BodyPart.PartName, dbo.Size.SizeName, dbo.PlanTable.Efficiency, 
                      dbo.PlanTable.Capacity, dbo.PlanTable.PlanQty, dbo.Order_Info.ShipmentDate, dbo.PlanTable.OrderQty, dbo.PlanTable.SAM, dbo.PlanTable.ActualQty, 
                      dbo.Machine_Info.Status AS MachineStatus
FROM         dbo.Machine_Info RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.PlanTable ON dbo.Machine_Info.MachineNo = dbo.PlanTable.MachineNo LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Style RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Order_Info ON dbo.Style.Id = dbo.Order_Info.Style LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Size ON dbo.Order_Info.Size = dbo.Size.Id ON dbo.PlanTable.OrderID = dbo.Order_Info.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.BodyPart ON dbo.Order_Info.BodyPart = dbo.BodyPart.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Buyer ON dbo.Order_Info.Buyer = dbo.Buyer.Id
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[OrderDetailsView]    Script Date: 03/18/2019 17:23:12 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[OrderDetailsView]
AS
SELECT     dbo.Order_Info.Id AS OrderID, dbo.Buyer.BuyerName, dbo.Style.StyleName, dbo.Size.SizeName, dbo.Dia.Dia, dbo.BodyPart.PartName, dbo.Order_Info.Buyer AS BuyerID, 
                      dbo.Order_Info.Style AS StyleID, dbo.Order_Info.Size AS SizeID, dbo.Order_Info.Dia AS DiaID, dbo.Order_Info.BodyPart AS PartID
FROM         dbo.Order_Info LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.BodyPart ON dbo.Order_Info.BodyPart = dbo.BodyPart.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Size ON dbo.Order_Info.Size = dbo.Size.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Dia ON dbo.Order_Info.Dia = dbo.Dia.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Style ON dbo.Order_Info.Style = dbo.Style.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Buyer ON dbo.Order_Info.Buyer = dbo.Buyer.Id
GO

/****** Object:  View [dbo].[LoadWithActualQtyView]    Script Date: 03/18/2019 17:23:12 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE VIEW [dbo].[LoadWithActualQtyView]
AS
SELECT     TOP (100) PERCENT dbo.PlanTable.TaskDate, dbo.PlanTable.MachineNo, dbo.PlanTable.OrderID, dbo.PlanTable.PlanQty, dbo.PlanTable.ActualQty, dbo.PlanTable.OrderQty, dbo.Buyer.BuyerName, 
                      dbo.Style.StyleName, dbo.Size.SizeName, dbo.Dia.Dia AS DiaName, dbo.BodyPart.PartName
FROM         dbo.BodyPart RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Order_Info ON dbo.BodyPart.Id = dbo.Order_Info.BodyPart LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Dia ON dbo.Order_Info.Dia = dbo.Dia.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Size ON dbo.Order_Info.Size = dbo.Size.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Style ON dbo.Order_Info.Style = dbo.Style.Id LEFT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.Buyer ON dbo.Order_Info.Buyer = dbo.Buyer.Id RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                      dbo.PlanTable ON dbo.Order_Info.Id = dbo.PlanTable.OrderID
ORDER BY dbo.PlanTable.TaskDate, dbo.PlanTable.OrderID
GO
